 

Task 1:
For different lists of SNPs covered by different assays, group alleles into indistinguishable allels.    
TODO: Compare that to alleles claimed to be discoverable by manufacturer.




** ASSAY: hypothetical_assay_covering_all_rsids_in_pharmgkb **
3 set(s) of mutually indistinguishable haplotypes:  [{'*2', 'H1', 'H2', 'H5'}, {'*3', 'H7'}, {'H3', '*1', 'H6'}]
10 rsids were used to define haplotypes for this gene


** ASSAY: dmet_plus **
3 set(s) of mutually indistinguishable haplotypes:  [{'H8', '*3', 'H7'}, {'*2', 'H1', 'H2', 'H5'}, {'H3', '*1', 'H6'}]
7 rsids were used to define haplotypes for this gene


** ASSAY: florida_stanford_chip **
3 set(s) of mutually indistinguishable haplotypes:  [{'H8', '*3', 'H7'}, {'H9', '*1', '*4', 'H3', 'H4', 'H6'}, {'*2', 'H1', 'H2', 'H5'}]
3 rsids were used to define haplotypes for this gene


** ASSAY: veracode_adme_corepanel **
2 set(s) of mutually indistinguishable haplotypes:  [{'*3', 'H8', 'H9', '*1', '*4', 'H3', 'H4', 'H6', 'H7'}, {'*2', 'H1', 'H2', 'H5'}]
1 rsids were used to define haplotypes for this gene


** ASSAY: taqman **
1 set(s) of mutually indistinguishable haplotypes:  [{'*2', '*3', 'H8', 'H9', '*1', '*4', 'H1', 'H2', 'H3', 'H4', 'H5', 'H6', 'H7'}]
0 rsids were used to define haplotypes for this gene
 

Task 2:
For different lists of SNPs covered by different assays, calculate how many samples in 1000genomes would be assigned an allele 
that actually does not match the 'correct' allele ('correct' allele = the allele inferred based on 'hypothetical_assay_covering_all_rsids_in_pharmgkb').
